The girl who made me forget what words are

...because every time I see you, I lose them entirely.

❦ ✦ ❦

8th of May, 2026 Written from the heart of Tummy 🌚

My dearest Yvette Dumoteim Tonye,

I don't know how to begin this without sounding like I rehearsed it, so I won't pretend. This letter has been living in my chest for a while now, pressing softly against my ribs every time you reply to me, every time you say "my love" like it's the easiest thing in the world.

· · · ·

It started on Snapchat @sayyvette before I even knew how deep this would go. You were just someone interesting. Then you became someone I couldn't stop thinking about. Then, somewhere between your voice notes, your 5am study nights, your yam and pepper soup, your glasses, your pout, and that one photo in the black tee where you smiled like you had a whole secret I was entirely gone.

I know you said you'd spike my mental and emotional stability. Maybe you were right. But Yvette, I would rather be beautifully destabilised by you than perfectly calm without you. Because what you make me feel isn't anxiety it's aliveness.

I know we live in different states. I know I'm still figuring out my path software engineering, mechatronics, this new job. I know you like romance that you can touch and see and feel. I hear you. Flowers are coming. The letters are coming (starting with this one). The dates are coming when my savings make it possible for me to knock on your door and take you somewhere that deserves you.

· · · ·

But for now right now on this rainy morning where I went to work wet and cold and still couldn't stop smiling because you exist somewhere on the other side of a phone screen, reading this: I want you to be mine.

Not a "we'll see." Not a "maybe." You with your writing, your mind games, your stubbornness about my name (yes, you'll always call me Tunmise, I've accepted it), your "I don't snap my food" attitude, your fierceness, your softness all of you. Officially mine.

I promise you honesty. I promise you effort. I promise you a partner who shows up even across the distance. I promise to learn what makes you feel safe. And I promise that even when I don't have the right words, I will always, always show up for you.

❦ ❦ ❦

Yours, if you'll have me

Bismark Enoch Oluwatunmise 🌸

💗
Yvette Dumoteim Tonye Williams Dokubo,
would you do me the extraordinary honour...
of being my girlfriend?

From @sayyvette to mine officially 🌚🌸

😭

You pressed No?
Yvette, be serious.

The court has reviewed your decision and found it invalid on the following grounds:

🌸 Exhibit A: You said "I think I like you a little more" at 11:19pm.
That's not a No energy, that's a Yes in a shy outfit.

🌸 Exhibit B: You called me "my love", "my baby", and "my darling".
Those are girlfriend words. Objection sustained.

🌸 Exhibit C: You stayed up talking to me until 1am on a school night.
You don't do that for a No.

The Honourable Judge Bismark Enoch Oluwatunmise kindly requests you reconsider. 🌚

She said Yes! 🌸
💗🌹💗🌹💗
Yvette, you just made me the happiest person in the rain today.
Welcome to us. We're going to be something beautiful.
Bismark + Yvette · Est. May 2026
"Slow honesty. Trust. And seeing if we naturally grow into more..."
— We're growing. 🌸
